  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/7933543-gnome-claire-wishes-she-was-as-cool-as-gnome-ann"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1473246053i/7933543._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/7933543-gnome-claire-wishes-she-was-as-cool-as-gnome-ann">Gnome Claire *Wishes she was as cool as Gnome Ann*</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">you've probably already read it or not by now but I'd say this is one of the less standalone books from the series- Kaleb has been quite a big charact<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">you've probably already read it or not by now but I'd say this is one of the less standalone books from the series- Kaleb has been quite a big character since book 2 and we've been getting more and more hints about his story so if you read it first you'd miss that build up. I also don't know how well the world would make sense without the world development that's in the previous books.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_468995797" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468995797" />
    <a title="Lila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6659789-lila"><img alt="Lila" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426228692p2/6659789.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468995797?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lila" href="/user/show/6659789-lila">Lila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=chilling">chilling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=great-mc">great-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=all-nighter">all-nighter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=bad-ass">bad-ass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6659789-lila?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468995797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14105115034679418150"><br/>5 stars read for me<br/><br/><i>
  <b>What would you do if you were loved by most dangerous man in existence....?</b>
</i><br/><br/>I'll be honest with you- although, romance in all previous books in series was lovely, I was driven by story in the background. Story about Silence, rebellion, upcoming civil war. If you are like me, let me tell you upfront, Heart of Obsidian is <b>that</b> book; it's the book where all the questions are answered. Isn't it ironic that at the same time I find this novel to be the most romantic in series...?</span>
  <span id="freeText14105115034679418150" style="display:none"><br>5 stars read for me<br><br><i>
  <b>What would you do if you were loved by most dangerous man in existence....?</b>
</i><br><br>I'll be honest with you- although, romance in all previous books in series was lovely, I was driven by story in the background. Story about Silence, rebellion, upcoming civil war. If you are like me, let me tell you upfront, Heart of Obsidian is <b>that</b> book; it's the book where all the questions are answered. Isn't it ironic that at the same time I find this novel to be the most romantic in series...?<br>In its core, Heart of Obsidian is a simple love story between two people who are anything but simple. When I finally found out who the hero is I was beyond happy. Kaleb is one character who intrigued me since we first met him in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/215643.Visions_of_Heat__Psy_Changeling___2_" title="Visions of Heat (Psy-Changeling, #2) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Visions of Heat</a> and I don't know if I ever read about character that is so ambiguous and captivating at the same time (maybe Barrons.) We were hinted in previous installments that Kaleb is beautiful and that he has immense power, but true force of both those statements we come to see in HoO. I finished this book completely in love with Kaleb and I can say he is by far my favorite character (sorry Judd, I loved you for a very long time). Kaleb is so beautiful and perfect in his Silence, and yet inside he is a man so damaged, complex and troubled. What Kaleb had to survive and what it did to him made me want to scream and hug him (like he would let that ;)) and never let go. Oh, how wrong were Psy for initiating Silence Protocol! Kaleb, the most perfect of them all is at the same time clear evidence of "wrongness" that Silence is.<br>This is perfect place to make connection with other big secret of this series and I won't spoiled it if you don't want to know. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[As soon as I was in Kaleb's head and learned more about the way he thinks, I don't know how could I ever think that Ghost can be anyone else but him. It seemed so logic and understandable and I must hand it to Nalini- She worked us masterly.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>As for heroine- Sahara was everything you expect a right woman for Kaleb to be. She is brave, strong, emphatic, sensible and she is fierce! She deserved such devotion and loyalty from Kaleb imo. No TSTL moments for Sahara... I really liked her big time. I'm hoping we get to see her more using her ability in next books, it was very interesting. <br>Sex scenes- Oh. My. God. I want a Tk-Psy for me. That is all. Whenever there is a discussion about hottest sex scenes we ever read, I always mentioned Judd scene in CbI... but Kaleb? Off the chart hot.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/615244.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know different reviewers mentioned different books in series, so I'll say that HoO reminds me one part of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6353014.Blaze_of_Memory__Psy_Changeling___7_" title="Blaze of Memory (Psy-Changeling, #7) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Blaze of Memory</a>, one part of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/458034.Caressed_by_Ice__Psy_Changeling___3_" title="Caressed by Ice (Psy-Changeling, #3) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Caressed By Ice</a> and one part of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1830755.Mine_to_Possess__Psy_Changeling___4_" title="Mine to Possess (Psy-Changeling, #4) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Mine to Possess</a>.<br><br>The story ends at very unusual place: at the Beginning. At the beginning of new time for world Nalini Singh created and I can say it's fitting place to finish Kaleb' and Sahara's story. I can honestly say that I closed this book as a very satisfied reader. Also, having my answers on questions that tormented me for years, my interest in this series didn't flail. I want to read about aftermath of events in HoO and how it affected all three races. I trust Nalini enough to know she's going to deliver great story. I recommend entire series wholeheartedly. <br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14105115034679418150" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1131565014" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1131565014" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131565014?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101605196" href="/book/show/15985353-heart-of-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-p-z">authors-p-z</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131565014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9808108096096149068"><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948964.gif' alt=' photo 115452cd-a771-45e3-860c-63f7a889f702_zpse45a59f5.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote><br/>The 12th novel in Nalini Singh’s brilliant Psy/Changeling Series, set in the complex, dark and fantastic world that she has created. And the first book that features two Psy characters as a couple. Darkness & Light..<blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948965.jpg' alt=' photo images_zpsf88a9ba7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>A beautiful, intense, dark and emotionally filled love story, of two broken people meant to be together since they first met as children. Of how powerful love can be between two souls, despite the pain, the cruelty, the torture both endured nothing will keep them apart</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText9808108096096149068" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948964.gif" alt=" photo 115452cd-a771-45e3-860c-63f7a889f702_zpse45a59f5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>The 12th novel in Nalini Singh’s brilliant Psy/Changeling Series, set in the complex, dark and fantastic world that she has created. And the first book that features two Psy characters as a couple. Darkness &amp; Light..<blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948965.jpg" alt=" photo images_zpsf88a9ba7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A beautiful, intense, dark and emotionally filled love story, of two broken people meant to be together since they first met as children. Of how powerful love can be between two souls, despite the pain, the cruelty, the torture both endured nothing will keep them apart. <br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948966.jpg" alt=" photo images2_zpsa9add850.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> First introduced in Visions of Heat, Psy Councilor Kaleb Krychek is one of the most powerful, cold, dangerous, emotionless and ruthless members in the Psy Council<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948967.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mt6s511kx01rntrxvo1_500_zpsa40250a9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> who had been under the guidance of the evil, now dead, Psy Cardinal, Enrique Santano. Since a child, had been exposed to the most horrific world, that made him become the person he is today….icy and dark hearted…<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948968.jpg" alt=" photo download_zps4f0cc182.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> – he has no problem with killing his enemies and anyone who stands in his way in reaching his goals, one of those being in finding someone that disappeared from his life seven years ago, whose identify we learn at the end in Tangle of Need.<blockquote><b>Kaleb Krychek, cardinal telekinetic and a man no one wanted to meet alone on a dark night, had been searching for his quarry for seven years, three weeks, and two days. Even while he slept, his mind had continued to hunt through the sprawling psychic network that was the heartbeat and the cage of the Psy race. Not for a day, not for a second, had he forgotten his search, forgotten what they'd taken from him.<br>Everyone involved would pay. He'd make certain of it.</b></blockquote>
<br>Sahara Nightstar,<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948969.jpg" alt=" photo images1_zps4cd82afe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Faith Nightstar’s cousin who had disappeared seven years ago and had been held captive and tortured by one of the Council Members. The pain she endured and her mind almost erased was beyond belief.<br><br>A lot happens in this book. The world is a dangerous place for everyone – the struggle between the human race, Psy and Changeling world is about to implode. Things unravel at a breathtaking and neck-breaking pace, where secrets are revealed and lots of questions answered…one being the Ghost’s identity is….did we ever guess it?????.....well, it’s no biggie that it’s Kaleb K….I felt all along that there was a good side to him…he had a heart, he had a goodness that he had kept locked away all those years. We begin to see this as Sahara slowly shows him the light he has inside <br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948970.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n5t8qeCZ4v1ttux4xo1_500_zps95f29e19.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>
<b>What made this story so special for me:</b><br><br>Although the plot delves into the politics of the Psy/Changeling world, it does not detract from the love story of Kaleb &amp; Sahara. They are the main characters and feature in almost every chapter, giving you an insight into the healing and love of each other.<blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418924736ra/12948971.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_nbl488ZzHC1rrugpso1_500_zpsr3axxeip.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>
<br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948972.jpg" alt=" photo 0_zps959c3964.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>How love changed them both….Sahara’s love making Kaleb see the light inside of him….that he was not only darkness <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948973.jpg" alt=" photo 589a2ba8658619e56ec3dd1a70319c83_zpse63e5cd7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> That despite the pain and torture they had both endured, they complemented each other perfectly.<br><br>Absolutely brilliant how the author managed to make Kaleb into a likable character at the end, without making him into a “wimp”….he’s still dangerous, still loyal, still focused and still true to his goal in making the Psy world a better place for everyone. Hell, he will go to any ends to make Sahara happy, to care for her …<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948974.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n8mi3r7BlB1r4in83o1_500_zpsd9698e04.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>I loved meeting up with characters from the previous books………Faith Nightstar, Mercy, Judd and so many others…and the time Sahara spent in the Changeling world….<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948975.jpg" alt=" photo 45196853e70d3d7006eaa6b32aef48d9_zpsd42de804.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>Beautifully written, words that flow with such vividness that takes you into this incredible and imaginative world, draws you in to the lives of endearing, lovable and unforgettable characters.<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948976.jpg" alt=" photo 0913b2ee9480c4c31c0880ab9d2ffb94_zps38c2230b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>An absolute joy it was reading Kaleb and Sahara’s story.. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418924736i/12948977.jpg" alt=" photo download_zps05c1cc32.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="9808108096096149068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2680559611" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2680559611" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2680559611?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=superpowers-specialpowers">superpowers-specialpowers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2680559611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1177665278683898644">Kaleb Krychek and Sahara Nightstar. <br/><br/><i>Me: *finds the most psychotic, handsome and evil asshole in the series.*<br/>Me: “you are my new book boyfriend and I will love you until the ends of the earth.”</i><br/>Source: Facebook, Author: Unknown<br/><br/>Kaleb Krychek is psychotic, handsome and evil. And this book did everything to emphasise this fact:<br/><br/>1.	PSYCHOPATH <br/><i>Either she had never before met him and she was going mad, or their previous meeting had been so horrific, her mind protected her from it even now . . . kept her </i></span>
  <span id="freeText1177665278683898644" style="display:none">Kaleb Krychek and Sahara Nightstar. <br /><br /><i>Me: *finds the most psychotic, handsome and evil asshole in the series.*<br />Me: “you are my new book boyfriend and I will love you until the ends of the earth.”</i><br />Source: Facebook, Author: Unknown<br /><br />Kaleb Krychek is psychotic, handsome and evil. And this book did everything to emphasise this fact:<br /><br />1.	PSYCHOPATH <br /><i>Either she had never before met him and she was going mad, or their previous meeting had been so horrific, her mind protected her from it even now . . . kept her from realizing that she was at the mercy of a man groomed to adulthood by a psychopathic murderer.<br />“Did you help Enrique murder his victims?” she asked, the words torn out of her.<br />Kaleb’s eyes swirled with a blackness that seemed deeper than ebony as he shifted position so that he was looking down at her, his hand still at her throat. <b>“I,” he said, brushing his thumb over the flutter of her pulse, “was there for every second of their torture and deaths.”</b></i><br /><br />2.	HANDSOME<br /><i>With his black hair, cardinal eyes, and honed physique, Kaleb might be almost <b>shockingly handsome</b>, but the beauty was nothing but a mask for the deadly mind within.</i><br /><br />3.	EVIL<br /><i>“Tell me,” aware of a vast gulf beneath her feet, a storm of knowledge that pushed at her mind but couldn’t penetrate. “Tell me you aren’t evil.” Please.<br />Kaleb’s thumbs moved against her temples. “I’m sorry.”<br />Shaking her head in a mute refusal to accept what he was trying to tell her, she lifted trembling fingers to his jaw. <br /><b>“What have you done?”<br />“Too much that can never be undone.</b>”</i><br /><br /><b>Kaleb Krychek you are definitely my new book boyfriend and I will love you until the ends of the earth...</b><br /><br />But enough about me LOL<br /><br />The book is like a crossroad for the Psy community:<br />1.	Psys need to decide if the Silence is worthwhile.<br />2.	Psys need to have a new absolutely powerful leader who will lead them to the unknown.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1177665278683898644" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_524444389" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524444389?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Lioness" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Lioness" href="/user/show/4974909-lady-lioness">Lady Lioness</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4974909-lady-lioness?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4974909-lady-lioness?shelf=subgenre-psychic-powers">subgenre-psychic-powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4974909-lady-lioness?shelf=read-may-2013">read-may-2013</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524444389" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15596643910459662210">It had been over 365 days since I read a new full-length Psy-Changeling novel and I did my best to refrain from impatient whining. As a reward for my uncharacteristic, albeit reluctant, acceptance of delayed gratification, the Book Gods saw fit to grant me a boon. Enough about me, though, as I know you want to know about the book, so let's move on to the pretty-much-spoiler-free-because-it's-all-my-reactions review. <br/> <br/><u>Heart of Obsidian</u> reminds me of those long, quiet, hours that mark off time bef</span>
  <span id="freeText15596643910459662210" style="display:none">It had been over 365 days since I read a new full-length Psy-Changeling novel and I did my best to refrain from impatient whining. As a reward for my uncharacteristic, albeit reluctant, acceptance of delayed gratification, the Book Gods saw fit to grant me a boon. Enough about me, though, as I know you want to know about the book, so let's move on to the pretty-much-spoiler-free-because-it's-all-my-reactions review. <br /> <br /><u>Heart of Obsidian</u> reminds me of those long, quiet, hours that mark off time before night slips into the dawn. Change is happening, anything is possible, and a new day is breaking. Still, this is not an easy book. As much as one could claim the main theme is rebirth, there's no denying the traumas that perpetually ripple throughout the book. It will be a trigger for some, especially given recent events, and, by the end, parents may reconsider the wisdom of letting their teenagers fly too far from the nest. <br /> <br />Despite the heaviness, this is one of Nalini's simplest books. It could almost be a stand-alone, if the reader was familiar with the sociological and political framework of the Psy/Changeling world, as it focuses very tightly on the hero and heroine. The SnowDancers don't appear at all and only two of the previous heroines make cameos. However, just like I said in my <u>Tangle of Need</u> review, starting with <u>Heart of Obsidian</u> will do you a disservice. Nalini has brought together disparate threads to reveal a stunning tapestry that finally shows what she has been working towards during the past eleven books. There are clues as far back as <u>Slave to Sensation</u> and jumping to the end will rob you of the grand reveals. <br /> <br />With <u>Tangle of Need</u>, I was willing to cryptically answer questions, but I'm not going to do that with <u>Heart of Obsidian</u>. As I said previously, the book is so tightly focused, a hint about one thing could also apply to everything. so feel free to speculate in the comments, but I will not confirm or deny anything. However, I will tell you that my personal theory about the Ghost was very wrong. Oh, and the hero. I'll tell you the hero. <br /> <br />Don't click if you don't want to know. <br /> <br /> <br />Seriously. <br /> <br /> <br />Last chance to back away.<br /> <br /> <br />Here it comes. <br /><br /><i><b>Edited to Add</b>: Nalini has posted the first two chapters of <u>Heart of Obsidian</u> at her <a href="http://nalinisingh.blogspot.co.nz/2013/05/heart-of-obsidian-excerpt-spoiler-zone.html" target="new" rel="nofollow noopener">blog!</a>. </i> <br /> <br />I give you the first sentence of <u>Heart of Obsidian</u>: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["Kaleb Krychek, Cardinal telekinetic and a man no one wanted to meet alone on a dark night, had been searching for his quarry for seven years, three weeks, and two days."<br /><br />I know there are some die-hard Kaleb fangirls out there and you are going to be <i>very</i> happy. Nalini took a cryptic blank-slate-could-go-either-way character and turned him into a fascinatingly complex man. And, dayum, he's also scorchingly hot. There was one bit on page 131 that had me cranking up the AC. <br /><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>Heart of Obsidian</u> releases on June 4th. If you buy the e-book from Barnes and Noble, steeling yourself against Penguin's WTF ebook pricing, you should be able to download it around 1am on the 4th. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15596643910459662210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16897591114486343425"><b>WOW.</b><br/><br/>That's all that could come to mind as I read this. I have read every book in this series and have appreciated some more than others - the "others" I didn't love as much being those that didn't focus on a changeling as at least one of the main two characters. I'm not sure why, but I always found the chapters that focused on the Psy Council and related issues to be somewhat boring in comparison to the excitement and earthiness of the changeling world and characters? I'm not sure. Needless to s</span>
  <span id="freeText16897591114486343425" style="display:none"><b>WOW.</b><br /><br />That's all that could come to mind as I read this. I have read every book in this series and have appreciated some more than others - the "others" I didn't love as much being those that didn't focus on a changeling as at least one of the main two characters. I'm not sure why, but I always found the chapters that focused on the Psy Council and related issues to be somewhat boring in comparison to the excitement and earthiness of the changeling world and characters? I'm not sure. Needless to say, when I read the blurb about this book - as secretive and mysterious as it was - I had a feeling it would be all Psy--and it was. <br /><br />This made me nervous that I would not be into this one; however, I absolutely <i>LOVED</i> this book. I found it a little slow at the start, but once it got going, it was awesome. Nalini Singh can truly weave a story. Her Psy-Changeling world is such a magnificent construct and it all culminates in this installment. I don't want to reveal any spoilers, so I'll keep it short, but if you love this series you will love this book, the two main characters, and their journey. I am wondering if she will do anything more with it. She left potential for more... <br /><br /> </span>

<div id="review_465775941" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/465775941" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/465775941?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/179852-katie-babs?shelf=i-want-to-have-babies-with-the-book">i-want-to-have-babies-with-the-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer465775941&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer465775941" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4244054198085380191">Dear Nalini,<br/><br/>As you know I’m one of your biggest fans. I’ve read your Psy-Changeling series since the beginning, starting with Slave to Sensation, which is my all time favorite book in this series, although now Heart of Obsidian may tie for that spot. Sascha and Lucas will always hold a special place in my heart. You also know I'm a big fan girl (if not the biggest) for a specific character introduced in Visions of Heat, the second book. This is Kaleb Krychek, a deadly cardinal Tk and one of the </span>
  <span id="freeText4244054198085380191" style="display:none">Dear Nalini,<br /><br />As you know I’m one of your biggest fans. I’ve read your Psy-Changeling series since the beginning, starting with Slave to Sensation, which is my all time favorite book in this series, although now Heart of Obsidian may tie for that spot. Sascha and Lucas will always hold a special place in my heart. You also know I'm a big fan girl (if not the biggest) for a specific character introduced in Visions of Heat, the second book. This is Kaleb Krychek, a deadly cardinal Tk and one of the heads of the Psy Council who with a blink of an eye can kill a person where they stand. It wasn’t until Mine to Possess, book 4, where I started keeping a very close watch on Kaleb. I knew the moment he started sweating on a balcony in that book after an intense workout, I guess you should say my spidey senses tingled. I knew at one point Kaleb would be “reformed” and become one of your heroes at one point, although the consensus of your readers thought otherwise. I’ve waited 5 years for Kaleb to be in the spotlight. Finally his time has come in Heart of Obsidian.<br /><br />The main couple of Heart of Obsidian was kept under lock and key, which now I understand why. Revealing the main couple of this book would have many of your readers, including myself, throwing around speculations, specifically regarding the identity of the Ghost. For me, I was more concerned with how Kaleb would be portrayed than the Ghost (which is revealed in a very satisfactory way and had me guessing right up until the very last moment), and if you could give him and his heroine a worthy HEA like you’ve given all your prior couples. I’m pleased to say that Heart of Obsidian stopped my heart. You continue to get better with every single book you write. I would say Heart of Obsidian is your masterpiece of this series and quite possibly the best book of your career. My crush on Kaleb has changed into full blown awe and love for this man who has defied everything he is and all he has been taught all because of love. Kaleb’s goal and true meaning in life isn’t to destroy and kill because he was taught by a true sociopath whose goal was to make Kaleb into a cold blooded, heartless killer that even the Psy community would run away in fear of. Kaleb has spent the majority of his life in his own personal hell, which was shown at a very early age through flashbacks here. At the age of twelve he was learning to become ruthless and psychotic, but was able to remain human and keep those morals and feelings that go against his culture, all because of one little girl at the age of five who he meets and becomes friend with. She is Sahara NightStar, the Psy cousin to Faith (the heroine in Vision of Heat) who disappeared at the age of sixteen and is thought to be dead.<br /><br />The way you begin Heart of Obsidian is very crafty. We don’t know the name of the woman Kaleb has taken until around page fifty. All we know is that Kaleb has been searching for her for 7 years. She’s been abused, tortured and is near catatonic. Kaleb needs her to heal because he has specific plans for her. As what these plans are, all be revealed with a master stroke of writing. The way Kaleb treats this poor woman, who we come to know as Sahara, is incredibly tender. Kaleb’s one purpose in life is to keep Sahara away from all harm. He feels Sahara is his and no one ever again is going to take her from him. He lives and breathes revenge against those who have hurt his Sahara and he will make them pay.<br /><br />Eventually Sahara does heal because of Kaleb’s care and as she rebuilds her mind that she purposely shut down and becomes strong again. She has major memory loss and has no idea what Kaleb is to her. What she does know is that Kaleb is her protector and she isn’t afraid of him. Kaleb is concerned that when Sahara remembers her past and his part in her pain and suffering, she’ll reject him. If she does, he can’t go on living, and because of that he may destroy the Net that keeps his people-the Psy alive. Sahara holds the key to his salvation and his plans to create a harmonious future not just for his people, but for Sahara and himself.<br /><br />Nalini, I’ve said it before and I’ll say it again, you have a way with words and these characters of yours. Heart of Obsidian hit me deep in the gut and swept through my heart like a steam engine. I soaked up every word, every piece of dialogue. I can’t stop thinking about Kaleb’s and Sahara’s interactions. These two are pretty much the anti-Psy because of how strong they feel for one another. I was worried that a romance with two Psy wouldn’t work. We’ve seen one Psy find happiness with a changeling woman in Judd, but Kaleb here puts Judd to shame in the romance department, I’m afraid to say. The way Kaleb feels for Sahara, his hunger for her, is unlike any of your past heroes. Kaleb’s feelings for Sahara are so tangible I could taste it. I choked on it. I wanted to choke on it even more.<br /><br />Sahara might just be your strongest heroine of any you have created. She reminds me somewhat of Sasha in how she recovers from her trauma and wants to live and embrace all that life has to offer. She needs her freedom like the air she breathes and I love how Kaleb gave that to her without any question. I loved how she opened her mind, heart, body and soul to Kaleb because she just knew he was her safety net. Kaleb thinks he isn’t worthy of Sahara because of what he had to do to succeed and how he was forced to kill and hurt innocent people because of one sadistic individual, his deceased serial killer caretaker.<br /><br />Love indeed heals all wounds and Heart of Obsidian is an example of this. It's an epic romance. Kaleb and Sahara’s love is poetic and breathtaking, including steamy and sexy. The love scenes crackle, and how Kaleb literately made the earth move for Sahara when they were intimate was a nice payoff.<br /><br />I would say Heart of Obsidian completes the main story arc you set for this series. It’s very well played, and yet I want more. Kaleb and Sahara’s HEA is pure gold. This is one book that I will hold close to my chest and bow down to its creator because it’s that good and embodies what a true romance should be. Take a bow, you deserve it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4244054198085380191" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11422819842051986669">First time read: March 28th 2015<br/>Second re-read: December 25th 2016<br/>_____________________________________<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461184423ra/18835586.gif' width='400' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is one of my all time favourites!!! I love Kaleb, I love Sahara and I freaking love everything about their story!!! It's such an amazing journey these two go through. Not all is pretty but therefore so much worth it at the end. I really like the plot, it's not like the previous books. We basically get the story of just Sahara and Kaleb, without the unnecessary side stories of other ch</span>
  <span id="freeText11422819842051986669" style="display:none">First time read: March 28th 2015<br>Second re-read: December 25th 2016<br>_____________________________________<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461184423ra/18835586.gif" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is one of my all time favourites!!! I love Kaleb, I love Sahara and I freaking love everything about their story!!! It's such an amazing journey these two go through. Not all is pretty but therefore so much worth it at the end. I really like the plot, it's not like the previous books. We basically get the story of just Sahara and Kaleb, without the unnecessary side stories of other characters. That's probably a huge reason why I love the story so much. Also, it's a shorter book than the rest of them, thankfully. I felt like the previous books had so much other stuff going on that I couldn't really enjoy the main story of these two characters. But in this book the plot is awesome and we truly get to see basically just their story. Also, we finally get some huge answers answered, yes! I think this could've been easily the last book in this series because it's perfect! <br><br>We met Kaleb in previous books and he always came across as this cold, unapproachable psy with unlimited power. He seemed to have the perfect Silence. But in this story, we get to see his other side that he only shows to Sahara and it's sooooo beautiful how much he cares for her and how he's with her. He waited a long time for them to be together in a room again. I'm so happy for him. <br><br>As for Sahara's character, she a very smart and strong woman but also super loyal. I loved how she was with Kaleb, they really deserved each other. Such a strong and amazing couple!<br><br>I'm not giving anything away plot wise but all I can say is is that it's awesome! You won't regret reading this story! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13891184893302587672"><b>*** 4.25 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with my girls @ BB&B!!!</b><br/><br/>He is the Superman of the Psy and she is the strong but broken girl who has loved him for a very long time.... He is the most powerful weapon in the Net, she is the only one who could rain him in. He had been looking for her for a long time, ever since she had been stolen from him and hidden from the Net and society. Now he has her back and nothing and no one will ever take her away from him again... Or the world would be in trouble!<br/><br/>Book 12 in the </span>
  <span id="freeText13891184893302587672" style="display:none"><b>*** 4.25 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with my girls @ BB&amp;B!!!</b><br /><br />He is the Superman of the Psy and she is the strong but broken girl who has loved him for a very long time.... He is the most powerful weapon in the Net, she is the only one who could rain him in. He had been looking for her for a long time, ever since she had been stolen from him and hidden from the Net and society. Now he has her back and nothing and no one will ever take her away from him again... Or the world would be in trouble!<br /><br />Book 12 in the Psy-Changeling Universe and Nalini Singh is still going strong! The main character in this story is one of the most interesting and intense Pay we have met yet and his book was almost destined to be wonderful, just based on the way we have been learning about him since the beginning of the series. And boy did it deliver!!! We are not left disappointed .<br /><br />I don't really want to say anything about the plot, since finding everything out as you read is part of the fun. If you are a fan of Paranormal Romance, this series is something you have to check out. If you are a fan of the Psy-Changeling Universe, this book is a must read!!! I enjoyed it and am looking forward to continuing with the series - I need to know what happens with Silence!!!<br /><br />I wish you all Happy Reading and many more good books for your future!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13891184893302587672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146848982" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7201970581169477057"><br/><b>5 EPIC stars <3</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"He was the monster that stalked nightmare, and they both knew that."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Ruthless killer. Cold-blooded. Without mercy .. Without conscience. He was a monster. Damaged. Powerful. Fearful. He had no empathy. His only weakness was HER. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>Sahara Kyriakus</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181856._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"An unsheathed blade." <br/>What he had become the day she vanished."</b><br/><br/>For the last seven years, Kaleb was looking for the girl who meant everything to him. All his life, he has loved only one person and that's Sahara. Their bond was so str</span>
  <span id="freeText7201970581169477057" style="display:none"><br><b>5 EPIC stars &lt;3</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"He was the monster that stalked nightmare, and they both knew that."</i>
</b><br><br>Ruthless killer. Cold-blooded. Without mercy .. Without conscience. He was a monster. Damaged. Powerful. Fearful. He had no empathy. His only weakness was HER. <br><br><b>
  <i>Sahara Kyriakus</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181856._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"An unsheathed blade." <br>What he had become the day she vanished."</b><br><br>For the last seven years, Kaleb was looking for the girl who meant everything to him. All his life, he has loved only one person and that's Sahara. Their bond was so strong. So powerful. He could never let her go. He would do anything and everything to bring her back to him, and on his wake, he has left destruction and death for the ones who dared to take her away from him. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Sahara! I'll come for you! Survive! Survive for me!"</i>
</b><br><br>Councilor Kaleb Krychek is unfeeling, doesn't care or touch anyone, and won't let himself feel emotions. The only exception was Sahara. But she was gone. All he wanted was vengeance. He wanted the world to pay. And he had the power to erase the whole human race in the blink of an eye.<br><br><b>"Because I can."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181857._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For the past seven years, Sahara was in captivity. While her captors wanted to use her powers for their favor, Sahara found a way to escape. She was able to get lost in the deepest corners of her mind, where no one could harm her. Where she couldn't feel. Where no one could discover the nature of her true powers. During that time, she was tortured, her mind was violated, her memories faded, and all that remained was the shell of the sixteen girl she used to be. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181858._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the beginning, when he only brought her to his house, she didn't know who he was. she didn't remember him. For her, he was her capture. she was suspicious, afraid, entrusting and wary. But Kaleb didn't allow that. He wanted her. He wanted her to SEE HIM.<br><br><b>"Don't be afraid of me, Sahara." Bending his head, he spoke with his lips against hers, the contact igniting a thousand tiny lightning strikes in her blood. "I'd line the streets with bodies before I'd ever hurt you."</b><br><br>Slowly, she realized, this dark man, this cold-blooded killer means her no harm. Not only that, he CARES about her in ways she couldn't grasp.<br><br><b>"Am I so important to you?"<br>"Yes," he said. "You're everything." The entire reason for his existence."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181859._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"You matter to me."<br>So simple. So honest. So powerful.</b><br><br>When she start to fall for this enigma, it was so freaking EPIC! I felt every emotion. Every caress. Every stroke. Every stare. Every touch. <br><br><b>"Gripping the back of her neck, he tasted her so deep, she'd never forget the taste of him. <i>Mine</i>, he thought, <i>you are mine.</i>"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181860.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finally, she saw him. She cared for him. She loved him.<br><br><b>"Serial killer, mass murderer, there's not a name for the evil that lives inside me."<br>Jaw set and eyes fierce, she'd shaken her head. "I won't let the darkness have you."</b><br><br>Both together were EXPLOSIVE, and i mean it literately. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420148395ra/13181861.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>"So we literally made the earth move?</i> A slight pause, before Kaleb said, <i>I suggest we don’t engage in sex in populated areas."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181862._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story progressed slowly, like a pot cooking on a low flame until it reaches his boiling point. Their history was told in flashbacks all throughout the story. We got snips from a past, so dark, that it broke mt freaking hear. And there was a certain memory, buried in the depths of her mind, that was the reason that tore them apart. <br><br><b>"Always Sahara had seen him. And always she had refused to walk away. The last time, it had cost her seven years of her life. This time, he'd lay the world itself at her feet."</b><br><br>As a reader, I was so confused, and at the same time, so curious about what went wrong, what was the cause for their separation, and why Kaleb had feared so much that Sahara will remember what happened. All I'm gonna say is, when the memory had finally surfaced to her consciousness, it was nothing like I thought it would be...;)<br><br><b>"He would do things for he'd do for no one else, but while he'd empty the sky for her so she could spread her wings, fly, he would not set her free. She belonged to him, would always belong to him."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403699998i/10131748._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm not gonna give away anything more, because this book should be read without knowing too much. It adds to the air of mystery that surround their past.<br><br><b>"He'd always said yes to her, to the girl who had given him a sense of belonging, a sense of <i>home</i>. As she'd grown and realized where he went when he left her, what was done to him, those eyes had turned bruised. But never had she turned away from him, no matter how broken he was when he came to her."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181863._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book was amazing. The love story was EPIC. I've never read about a hero so dedicate to someone like Kaleb was. There was no limits to the lengths Kaleb would go to bring his love back, and keep her safe after. <b>And never, ever, let her go.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420148395i/13181864._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"You", he said, "are the single exception that rule." The oldest, deepest, most beautiful flaw in his Silence. "Without you, I would be a monster."</b><br><br>To say i loved it, would be the understatement of the year ;)<br><br><b>"Only you," he said, the vow a final one. "My fierce, intelligent, lovely Sahara who spit in a monster's eye."</b><br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101605196" href="/book/show/15985353-heart-of-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=abused-hero-or-and-heroine">abused-hero-or-and-heroine</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558278767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5830142522081173134">*WARNING: HERO's NAME AHEAD*<br/><br/><b>5 The Price Of Silence Stars<br/><br/><i>"We stand at a crossroads. The decisions we make will either save us, or end us."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412963i/812482.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The time has come for the Psy to make a stand. The Silence that they inflicted upon themselves, to leash their minds has crippled them. They will have to break these restraints, face the vastness of their powers and abilities and step into a world that will keep moving without them.<br/><br/>Silence though, is double edged sword and while muting their souls it is also th</span>
  <span id="freeText5830142522081173134" style="display:none">*WARNING: HERO's NAME AHEAD*<br><br><b>5 The Price Of Silence Stars<br><br><i>"We stand at a crossroads. The decisions we make will either save us, or end us."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412963i/812482.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The time has come for the Psy to make a stand. The Silence that they inflicted upon themselves, to leash their minds has crippled them. They will have to break these restraints, face the vastness of their powers and abilities and step into a world that will keep moving without them.<br><br>Silence though, is double edged sword and while muting their souls it is also the only answer, the only barrier between them and the darkness they are capable of. The last wall between them and insanity; their only chance at ruling the world. And the Pure Psy, a rogue radical fraction of fanatics, are determined to do so, even if it means murdering anyone that stands in their way.<br><br>Silence and darkness, hand in hand; They will either save or doom the world. There are degrees in silence and light within the stars, in night's darkest hour.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>♪♫Hello darkness, my old friend<br>I've come to talk with you again<br>Because a vision softly creeping<br>Left its seeds while I was sleeping<br>And the vision that was planted in my brain<br>Still remains<br>Within the sound of silence♪♫</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412963ra/812483.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In these times of turmoil and upheaval there is a man, that his actions will decide the fate of the world and his decisions will turn the tide. He will either rise as a tyrant or a leader of hope, but all these, depend on an abused woman and his heart that she holds in her small hands.<br><br><i>
  <b>If she demanded vengeance, he’d turn the world bloodred.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404481i/787100._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kaleb Krychek</b> is a man that can make the Earth tremble and people bow to his will. A madman's protege, the youngest Councilor, a dual Cardinal, a nightmare.<br><br>He has finally retrieved what he was looking for the last 7 years. He took back what was stolen from him. And this vulnerable woman who they tried to break and bend to their twisted will, a strong soul with a will of obsidian and a heart bigger than the sky, will have to guide him not to the light exactly, but to redemption and be his conscience. He isn't the monster that they all afraid, but sometimes to fight the darkness you have to turn into a shadow yourself.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412963i/812484._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't want to go into much detail about the plot, twists and the sheer brilliance that is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/71688.Nalini_Singh" title="Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Nalini Singh</a>'s mind and writing style. The climax of the story and the build up from the first book until this one, speaks in itself of consistency and amazingness.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412963ra/812485.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Weaving so many threads and emotions in this complex worldbuilding that she has achieved, without losing focus of the main couple and their heartbreaking story, so unique and beautiful. And always reminding us, that the most cold people are hiding a thunderstorm of feelings underneath.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384773ra/743412.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A sensual story about two people that should have been broken, but they were meant for greatness and allowed love to show them the way. Every touch, every breath brings them closer but it may tear them apart and make the world crumble under their power.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412963ra/812486.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Exciting, riveting, emotional, almost lyrical, suspenseful and everything we had ever hoped of this book, Mrs. Singh's teaches how a series should be treated with. Not for one moment, does she let the pace down; she delivers plot twist upon plot twist and this why I will keep reading about Psy, Changelings, the Forgotten and the Arrows for another 12 books!<br><br>Bravo!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/376160.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"We are Psy and we are capable of greatness. It is time to step out of the dark."</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406820ra/794124.gif" width="245" height="184" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14343399161748296306">This 12th book in the series is fantastic, Singh's engaging style, richly developed characters and plot mean this book is another gem.<br/><br/>This book is a rich tapestry of intensity, passion, strength and resilience. Finally we get Kaleb Krycheck's story and that of the Psy women, Sahara Nightstar, who saves him and the world from what he could be without her. In previous books we have been shown Kaleb as a powerful, cold, extremely dangerous and ruthless Psy Councilor, what we discover here is that y</span>
  <span id="freeText14343399161748296306" style="display:none">This 12th book in the series is fantastic, Singh's engaging style, richly developed characters and plot mean this book is another gem.<br /><br />This book is a rich tapestry of intensity, passion, strength and resilience. Finally we get Kaleb Krycheck's story and that of the Psy women, Sahara Nightstar, who saves him and the world from what he could be without her. In previous books we have been shown Kaleb as a powerful, cold, extremely dangerous and ruthless Psy Councilor, what we discover here is that yes he is extremely dangerous and ruthless in his focus but cold he is not.<br /><br />This is a book you won't regret picking up and one you'll hate to put down until you're finished. It's certainly part of my re-read collection.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6761211823071180273"><b>WOW 5 mind BLOWING stars!</b><br/><br/>No name spoilers here...in case anyone is still waiting to read this book :)<br/><br/>This left me thinking, how much better can this series get after this? What story can truly top this off? I really didn't expect what I read, it surprised me at how something that was impossible could still be possible. Had me thinking no matter how broken, lost or unrecoverable a person can be, they should never give up in the face of love.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>His own hand was big, warm against her cheek as he cu</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText6761211823071180273" style="display:none"><b>WOW 5 mind BLOWING stars!</b><br><br>No name spoilers here...in case anyone is still waiting to read this book :)<br><br>This left me thinking, how much better can this series get after this? What story can truly top this off? I really didn't expect what I read, it surprised me at how something that was impossible could still be possible. Had me thinking no matter how broken, lost or unrecoverable a person can be, they should never give up in the face of love.<br><br><i>
  <b>His own hand was big, warm against her cheek as he cupped her jaw. "Don't be afraid of me." Bending his head, he spoke with his lips against hers, the contact igniting a thousand tiny lightning strikes in her blood. "I'd line the streets with bodies before I'd ever hurt you."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410083ra/803583.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"You are here," he said in a tone that made her heart thump wildly against her ribs, "because you belong to me."</b>
</i><br><br>The love story shared in this book, was truly beautiful to read about. It was highly emotional and heartwarming to be apart of their journey at finding their lost love. <br><br>Its so heartbreaking to have to go through such torture and sacrifices, just to be with the one you love, the one you only exist for, the one that holds you back from truly losing your humanity. To feel so much love for someone that you'd destroy everything, even yourself, for just the thought of losing them. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410083i/803584._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>
  <b>All she wanted to do was strip herself to the skin and wrap herself around him so close that nothing could ever separate them again.</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410083i/803585._SY540_.jpg" width="290" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Feeling their loses and gains as if they were my own, had me rooting for their well deserved HEA. The chemistry and connection shared between them was simply *sigh* AMAZING!<br><br><i>
  <b>You're mine," Simple quiet words that were a punch to the chest. "I will fight for you, today, tomorrow, and all the tomorrows to come."<br><br>"It will break my heart if you were hurt."</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410083i/803586._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>He felt something inside him that was so gentle it was painful.<br><br>"Why aren't you afraid of me if you remember? Why are you still here?" <br>"Because you're mine."<br><br>"I want us to fly together."</b>
</i> <br><br>The story line was highly intriguing and had me hooked and wondering what will happen next all the way. I HIGHLY recommend this book and series to all PNR fans. YOU HAVE TO READ IT! <br><br>It feel like this series, at book 12, has just begun.<br><br><i>
  <b>It is time to step out of the dark.</b>
</i> <br></span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386232i/745631._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Me, at the end of the book: please, don't end!</span>

    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/465757674?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=for-fresh-fiction-review">for-fresh-fiction-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer465757674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16444729529534096541">There has been so much hype surrounding the 12th book in Nalini Singh’s Psy-Changeling series. With the identity of the hero and heroine kept under wraps until the book was released, readers have been on edge with anticipation as speculations reached a whirlwind of activity. <br/><br/>Singh had a major challenge on her hands. The big reveal could either blow readers away with her ingenious plan or it could become a major disappoint. However, had there ever been a doubt to Singh’s talent? A master of lyric</span>
  <span id="freeText16444729529534096541" style="display:none">There has been so much hype surrounding the 12th book in Nalini Singh’s Psy-Changeling series. With the identity of the hero and heroine kept under wraps until the book was released, readers have been on edge with anticipation as speculations reached a whirlwind of activity. <br /><br />Singh had a major challenge on her hands. The big reveal could either blow readers away with her ingenious plan or it could become a major disappoint. However, had there ever been a doubt to Singh’s talent? A master of lyrical words and quiet, but intense emotions, Singh pens an epic masterpiece with the latest installment to the series. Readers will be floored not only by the reveal of the characters, but also by its lyrical detail and its heart-stopping emotions. HEART OF OBSIDIAN stands as one of the best books Singh has penned in her career.<br /><br />Attention to detail is what Singh prevails in. Each page, each word is necessary in building a vivid, dramatic picture. The main characters are hauntingly real and claw into your heart with their broken pasts. Action on a level you’ve never seen before in this series takes this book from good to stellar. I felt that Singh poured her whole soul into the pages of this book. You can feel her heartbeats pulsing on the page. <br /><br />In a dramatic and satisfying serving, HEART OF OBSIDIAN not only surpassed my high expectations, but Singh has ruined me for all other books. Passion on this level cannot be easily redone or replicated. Only Singh holds that power to blend lethal power and restrained passion and make it work. <br /><br /><b>Reviewed for<a href="http://freshfiction.com/review.php?id=37925" rel="nofollow noopener"> Fresh Fiction</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16444729529534096541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Still...<br/><br/><b>The hero</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426276i/851626.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What can I say about the "Obsidian" male? He is definitely in </span>
  <span id="freeText8080635311659243600" style="display:none">This book was so awesome. It's definitely in my top 3 in the series.<br><br>Since I enjoyed this system on my previous review I will use it again to make clear what I like about this book the most!<br><br> The couple: ★★★★★<br> The heroine: ★★★★★★★★★★<br> The hero: ★★★★★★★<br> The plot: ★★★★★<br>The limited POVS: ★★★★★<br> Aden &amp; Vasic: ★★★★★<br><br><br>I won't name the heroes although I'm pretty sure there aren't many people who haven't heard who they are anymore. Still...<br><br><b>The hero</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426276i/851626.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say about the "Obsidian" male? He is definitely in my top ten list of book heroes as of now. He is sexy, powerful, ruthless and loyal to a single woman. For her he would destroy the world(literally) but for her he would also save it. His love for the heroine doesn't make him "soft", just makes him think hard before being doing something bad! I LOVED him. I have a think for anti-heros and bad boys and he is certainly both but the heroine gives him a conciense or more accurately she IS his consciense. I am tempted to fight Ang for rights over him.<br><br><b>The heroine</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426276i/851627._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now the heroine was the best thing in this book. She was beyond the good mark. The girl was such a beautiful surprise. After being imprisoned for 7 years and treated like an animal she has the strength to go on with her life, to be thankful for the things she got back, to forgive the ones who harmed her, to dance with the most frightening man in the world. I respect her strength of character and loved the fact that she didn't have one whiny comment, one self-pitying instant. She was exactly what I like in my heroines, gutsy, brave, forgiving, compassionate and <b>so damn strong</b>. I would recommend this book to everyone just based on her.<br><br><br>The story was nice. Especially the romance related stuff. I enjoyed how their love grew and developed over the years and how they never lost their faith in each other even when the heroine couldn't remember anything of her life. Such a beautiful love story!<br><br>The plot in general was interesting. I liked the hero's displays of power and the way the heroines good nature made him a better person. I kind of liked the way the "war" progressed <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and the Pure Psy were defeated although I wanted Vasquez to suffer more(muaha haha). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But this was no surprise. Nalini Singh has proven many times that she knows how to write an arresting book and this is one of her best.<br><br>This book is definitely a 5 and I certainly forget many things I wanted to adress in my review but for now that's all!;)<br><br><b>1st re-read 26/08/2014</b><br><br>This book only gets better. I have so much respect for the heroine. The second time only added to it.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ren Puspita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ren Puspita" href="/user/show/3666031-ren-puspita">Ren Puspita</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">All Psy Changeling fans</span></div>
