        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer501850983" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1781242481374172163"><b>4,5 stars</b><br/><br/>Read my review in Indonesian on my little blog here: <br/><br/><a href='http://renslittlecorner.blogspot.com/2014/05/review-heart-of-obsidian-oleh-nalini.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393549803i/8730141._SX540_.png' alt='Ren's Little Corner' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book give me so many <b>FEELING.</b><br/><br/>Firstm, I'm so ashamed to admit that recently I'm so hot headed, so stubborn for delaying to read Heart of Obsidian. WHY? Because I'm so pissed off when reading any spoiler about who The Ghost was and it spoiled my excitement when the book finally come in my hand.<br/><br/>But then, after reading, I keep in my mind that the core of Heart of Obsidian was not <b>who is The Ghost?</b>, because his real identity is no</span>
  <span id="freeText1781242481374172163" style="display:none"><b>4,5 stars</b><br><br>Read my review in Indonesian on my little blog here: <br><br><a href="http://renslittlecorner.blogspot.com/2014/05/review-heart-of-obsidian-oleh-nalini.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393549803i/8730141._SX540_.png" alt="Ren's Little Corner" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book give me so many <b>FEELING.</b><br><br>Firstm, I'm so ashamed to admit that recently I'm so hot headed, so stubborn for delaying to read Heart of Obsidian. WHY? Because I'm so pissed off when reading any spoiler about who The Ghost was and it spoiled my excitement when the book finally come in my hand.<br><br>But then, after reading, I keep in my mind that the core of Heart of Obsidian was not <b>who is The Ghost?</b>, because his real identity is no longer matter to me. Heart of Obsidian is a story about two lost souls, two wounded hearts, two broken human beings who finally pass their obstacles and do not want to give up into each other. A story about a dual cardinal Psy and also Councilor with eyes so dark like a midnight sky named Kaleb Krychek and a woman who will make him destroy the world just to see her happy, Sahara Kyriakus.<br><br>This book started so slow, and the mystery is too deep, make me confused and frustated to know what exactly going on between that two. I also deeply disturbed by Kaleb's behavior to Sahara in the first part. His dominance make me scream, make me <b> "I don't want to read another alpha male that do not respect the heroine!"</b>, also Sahara seems like a meek woman. Yet, as the story unraveled, as we venture deep into Kaleb and Sahara's relationship and their past, all his demeanor and Sahara's act to him made sense. Made me understand Kaleb, a broken man with broken mind and soul, yet still fight for what he considered as his. Sahara too, not a damsel in distress. She seems so weak at first because of her captivity, yet in the end she show her strength. I applause Nalini for handled this sensitive (for me!) topic with grace and her beautiful writing style.<br><br>Oh, did I forget to tell you that Nalini's prose and words are so beautiful, sometimes it make your heart ache? That's what happen to me after read Heart of Obsidian. While Kaleb and Sahara's revelation of love sometimes can be too cheesy and over the top, sometimes I ached for them both. I'm jealous for Sahara, for have a man that soooo devoted to her. That Kaleb not hesitant to bring the world to its ending, tear it apart, if anything bad happen to her. Such a loyalty! Such a quality that I rarely found in romance novels that had so many overused theme, if you get my meaning.<br><br>Last, ahhh, I don't know what to said anymore, except if you not read Heart of Obsidian, READ IT ASAP! Buy your copy, or borrow it in library. If you already had it, don't make mistake like me. To neglect this book and missed a beautiful love story. <br><br>And, congrats for Heart of Obsidian to won Romantic Times Reviewers Award for Paranormal Romance category. I know that this book deserve it. Another keeper for sure!<br><br>For my early opinion and guess about this book, you can see it in this spoiler. Contain so many amused thing, I'm assured you :)<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>UPDATE</b><br>Nalini just posted two first chapter of Heart of Obsidian, and yes, I refuse to read it. I also refuse to read the first review of HoO posted in Goodreads, since it's way to kill my joy to read the book unspoiled. Also resist to read any Nalini Singh's interview on the blog world about this book. Yep, I'm stubborn like that, lol!<br><br>But today, I can't finally resist to follow The Ghost hijacking Nalini Singh's twitter, answer some question about him. I believe he do it unwillingly and still full of secrecy. This is what I gather from his (?) tweets :<br><br>- He doesn't understand with friendship concept, even Judd and Xavier believe they are friend.<br>- He has no family, but related to someone we have met, but the relationship is unknown by others. The relative is male. He will not answer further question about his lineage.<br>- For him, loyalty is everything, that's why he trust Judd, because Judd loyal to his family. He will not betray Judd and Xavier (awww!)<br>- His identity may or may not shock readers. Depend on how we see him (I will not shocked!). <br>- He does not have tattoo (yes!)<br>- Two characters know about his identity , one might be Judd. Since Ghost said, that man know who exactly he is.<br>- The Ghost considered using Sienna for his plan and no, he's not related to her. He also avoid question about Arrow<br>- The Ghost have touchy feeling about marriage (lol!), decline any marriage proposal from readers!<br>- The Ghost is.. virgin!! (woohoo). He never had sex, but it's a tool he will use if necessary.<br>- He had broken when he was child.<br>- His loyalty is to a woman, and his plan seems for this woman too, a woman he met when he was broken.<br><br>Now I will imagine Benedict Cumberbatch as Ghost. Yess, he will be perfect Ghost!<br><br>+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++<br><br>Whoever Ghost is (Kaleb, Vasic, etc)... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404481i/787099.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><s>Somebody, please bribe Nalini with chocolate or something sweet so she will spill some secret on this book.</s><br><br>Cover and title revealed!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379785017i/464576._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some speculation about this book :<br><br>The cover remind me of Star Trek Into Darkness movie poster<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404481i/787100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, the hero might be The Ghost, with the candicate are Kaleb, Vasic or Aden (based on discussion on Nalini Singh fans Goodreads Group). <br><b>Why its Ghost?</b><br>There's some passage from Kiss of Snow that mention about "Obsidian" (thanks, Lulu!):<br><br><b>From Kiss of Snow:<br>"That left him with the Obsidian archive. Created by the NetMind, the neosentience that was the guardian and librarian of the Net, the Obsidian archive was a backup in case the PsyNet ever suffered a catastrophic failure. The Ghost had named it Obsidian because the complexity of data within it made it all but a wall of black. Only a rare few individuals had ever realized the Obsidian archive existed. Even fewer knew how to access it." </b><br><br>According to one of readers, its from Kaleb's POV. So, Kaleb maybe not Ghost? I believe that Ghost is male, since the cover have man on it. Beside, based on the similarity with Star Trek movie poster (ehm, I don't know if Nalini is Trekkie or not *cough*) which there's opinion that in Star Trek (I might be wrong) the character that played by Benerdict Cumberbatch is might be anti-hero, person who regret his wrong doing and become better. So, its can be Kaleb, can be Vasic, can be Aden. OR a new person we never know of?<br><br>And I think this one will feature Psy-Psy couple, yay!<br><br><br>Official Blurb will be revealed in March 2013!<br>Blurb is up!<br><br><i>Step into New York Times bestseller Nalini Singh’s explosive and shockingly passionate Psy-<br>Changeling world…<br><br>A dangerous, volatile rebel, hands stained<br>bloodred. <br><br>A woman whose very existence has been<br>erased.<br><br>A love story so dark, it may shatter the<br>world itself.<br><br>A deadly price that must be paid.<br><br>The day of reckoning is here.<br><br>From “the alpha author of paranormal<br>romance” (Booklist) comes the most highly<br>anticipated novel of her career—one that<br>blurs the line between madness and genius,<br>between subjugation and liberation,<br>between the living and the dead. </i><br><br>Ugh, this blurb is not explain anything. But the hero become Ghost is true (and still hold possibilities between Kaleb or Vasic). And the heroine might be Alice. I mean, she had been comatose for a long time, right? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText3832554934277630203" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Don't be afraid of me." Bending his head, he spoke with his lips against hers, the contact igniting a thousand tiny lightning strikes in her blood. "I'd line the streets with bodies before I'd ever hurt you."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>11 books!<br>11 absolutely amazing, un-put-downable books. All leading up to book 12 that will absolutely, positively, blow.your.mind!<br><br>First, it's rare that you'll find a series that gets better with each new book. I read a lot of PNR, and I can count the authors that have been able to do that on one hand. Nalini Singh is one of those authors.<br><br>I have had my suspicions about this book, some have been true, some I was completely off on. What I do know, is that this book was<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402854ra/783426.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will not leave a full review, as I don't think I'll be able to do so without giving something away about HIM.<br><br>I will say this:<br><br>The writing:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402854ra/783427.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The love story:<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Why are you holding me?"<br>"Because you belong to me."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/599992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Beautiful, heart-breaking, emotional, AMAZING!</b><br><br><br>The plot:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402854ra/783428.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Nalini Singh<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/431655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR/UF Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167458-anna-bobs-her-hair?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632388623" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16800234561475076741"><b>Beautiful love story!...<u>(NO spoilers)</u></b><br/><br/>Avoid 'spoilery' reviews and just read the book! Discovering the answers as you read is a rewarding experience. All you need to know is Friendship, Loyalty, Kindness, and Love save the characters from devastation. <br/><br/>Psy romances don't really excite me (changelings rock my world) and I wasn't too eager for this book, BUT I loved the hero, heroine, setting, conflict, storytelling...EVERYTHING! It also didn't hurt that it contained one of my favorite tropes. (Not </span>
  <span id="freeText16800234561475076741" style="display:none"><b>Beautiful love story!...<u>(NO spoilers)</u></b><br /><br />Avoid 'spoilery' reviews and just read the book! Discovering the answers as you read is a rewarding experience. All you need to know is Friendship, Loyalty, Kindness, and Love save the characters from devastation. <br /><br />Psy romances don't really excite me (changelings rock my world) and I wasn't too eager for this book, BUT I loved the hero, heroine, setting, conflict, storytelling...EVERYTHING! It also didn't hurt that it contained one of my favorite tropes. (Not telling in this review.)<br /><br />This will be one of my favorite Psy/Changeling series rereads. It's <u>not</u> a story to be missed. Nalini Singh will keep you coming back for more after you read <i>Heart of Obsidian.</i> </span>

<div id="review_398499074" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/398499074" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/398499074?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101605196" href="/book/show/15985353-heart-of-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer398499074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5691819497917028903">4.5 ★'s <br/><br/>Finally, the book we've all been waiting for and the question we hope to get answered...is Kaleb Krychek The Ghost? Well, of course, I'm not going to tell you! But...I will tell you a few things. <br/><br/>First off let me just say that Nalini Singh can write like no other. I was blown away by how she wrote Kaleb and Sahara. Granted, she's written a few other good characters...okay, maybe <i>quite</i> a few other good characters, but these two are amazing! <br/><br/>I was a little hesitant about how two Psys would</span>
  <span id="freeText5691819497917028903" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s <br><br>Finally, the book we've all been waiting for and the question we hope to get answered...is Kaleb Krychek The Ghost? Well, of course, I'm not going to tell you! But...I will tell you a few things. <br><br>First off let me just say that Nalini Singh can write like no other. I was blown away by how she wrote Kaleb and Sahara. Granted, she's written a few other good characters...okay, maybe <i>quite</i> a few other good characters, but these two are amazing! <br><br>I was a little hesitant about how two Psys would work being together and having any type of passion but believe me, you don't have to worry about that. Both Kaleb and Sahara have had issues in the past that they've had to overcome and if you've been reading all the books in the series, you know how powerful Kaleb is and NS does not have weak heroines. Top that off with Kaleb and Sahara being childhood friends and you get a deeply emotional tie that defies Silence. <br><br>I do have to say that I did have a bit of a hard time with Kaleb. I <i>knew</i> he would be harder to warm up to than Judd...I just didn't realize how much. <b>Black Ice</b> is such an accurate term but I loved how he was being affected and what would happen! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793644i/580763.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sahara was wonderful...I liked her right from the get-go. Reading about how she treated Kaleb as a child just warmed my heart! The charms were one of my favorite parts and I loved all the stories behind them...that and the math and how she would bargain with him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793644i/580764.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though Kaleb and Sahara knew each other growing up and had feelings for each other, you can feel them falling even more in love. It did make me laugh when Kaleb lost a bit of control but I also loved seeing Sahara experiencing things. The "educational" videos were a hoot and just sooo something Kaleb would do. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/575169.gif" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a lot of history to go through and we do get to read about Sahara's family and her becoming friends with some of the other characters we already know. There are some really sweet scenes and one of my favorites that calls her "little sister". (I loved that!) I wished we had gotten more scene time from more characters but there really wasn't enough time. <br><br>Of course, there's all kinds of drama with the Pure Psy...a lot of 'explosive' scenes. I really liked seeing all the Psy, Changeling and Humans working together. It will be interesting to see where things go from here.<br><br>And...there was a hint of something possibly? between two Arrows. I'm not sure if anything will happen or not. It will be interesting to see where it goes from here and who the next book will be about! <br><br>And that question that I mentioned in the beginning...yes, it does get answered. <i>(But I'm still not telling you!!)</i> <br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ “You are here,” he said in a tone that made her heart thump wildly against her ribs, “because you belong to me.”<br><br>♥ "Some things need to be broken to become stronger."<br><br>♥ “I can feel you deep inside, a midnight star so impossibly strong and loving and <i>mine</i>.” Her voice trembled. “I’m so glad you’re mine. I won’t ever let you go.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="5691819497917028903" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_631882884" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/631882884" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/631882884?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer631882884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5948313084569508034">Move over Kiss of Snow. As much as I loved that book, Heart of Obsidian is even better. Easily and completely my new favorite in the Psy-Changeling series. I'm going to try very hard not to spoil the story beyond a basic set-up, but I am going to mention the hero and heroine by name, so beware.<br/><br/>Kaleb Krychek has been this powerful enigma ever since the series began. He is cold and calculating. But there is a fire under that ice that is positively molten. He has led a life shaped by cruelty at the</span>
  <span id="freeText5948313084569508034" style="display:none">Move over Kiss of Snow. As much as I loved that book, Heart of Obsidian is even better. Easily and completely my new favorite in the Psy-Changeling series. I'm going to try very hard not to spoil the story beyond a basic set-up, but I am going to mention the hero and heroine by name, so beware.<br /><br />Kaleb Krychek has been this powerful enigma ever since the series began. He is cold and calculating. But there is a fire under that ice that is positively molten. He has led a life shaped by cruelty at the hands of his mentor. He was brutalized. He never knew love or loyalty, until he met Sahara Nightstar. As children, they became the best of friends. She was his one solace... until she was ripped away. He has spent the past seven years searching for her. And now that he has her back, he will never let her go again.<br /><br />There is so much passion and emotion in this book. Kaleb's devotion to Sahara is so complete, so unbreakable, it's breathtaking. He is willing to do anything --give anything-- be anything-- for this fragile, abused woman. He would burn the world for her, and, frankly, he has the power to do it. His memories of her have shaped his entire life.<br /><br />Meanwhile, she has no memory of him at all. Years of torture have robbed her of so much, yet she knows him on a visceral level. She trusts him; she is drawn to him. And as she heals, she begins to remember him in bits and pieces.<br /><br />I love these two as individuals, but they are exponentially more amazing as a couple. What they bring out in each other is the very best part of the book. Their love is unconditional. They do not try to change each other. They simply are better people because of each other. Kaleb is no saint; he never has been. But Sahara doesn't expect him to be. She SEES him and loves him anyway... no --not in spite of who he is, but BECAUSE of it. He was forged in fire and it was what made him the man who owns her heart. It's her unflinching love of his true self that has changed his life; it is the delicate string that makes him a man instead of a monster.<br /><br />I could gush forever on the dynamic of the relationship... on how amazingly Nalini Singh crafted this bleak, unbending man who holds on to his humanity with the ray of hope created by one woman's regard. I could warn you to arm yourself with a fan to cool off from the OHMYGODHOT sex. But I would be remiss if I didn't also at least mention two other major points. One: We finally learn the identity of the Ghost and it's revealed in fabulous fashion. And two: the ending is huge. It will change the course of the series. It speaks to just how epic the romance is, however, that when the story is done, that's really all you'll be thinking about.<br /><br />I would not change a thing about this book. It was phenomenal. Go buy it right now.<br /><br />Rating: A+ <br /><br /><i>*ARC Provided by Berkley</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5948313084569508034" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_466152994" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/466152994" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466152994?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466152994" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17730099772164801619">There has been much build up and secrecy with this book in the months leading up to publication. Who is the hero? Who is the heroine? Is the Ghost involved? I’ve gone back and forth trying to figure out how to review this book and not give away answers to those who are trying to avoid spoilers. But at the same time, it’s hard to review a book when I can’t mention characters by name. So, I’ve decided to put the entire review under a spoiler tag. I don’t give away any major plot points or crazy sp</span>
  <span id="freeText17730099772164801619" style="display:none">There has been much build up and secrecy with this book in the months leading up to publication. Who is the hero? Who is the heroine? Is the Ghost involved? I’ve gone back and forth trying to figure out how to review this book and not give away answers to those who are trying to avoid spoilers. But at the same time, it’s hard to review a book when I can’t mention characters by name. So, I’ve decided to put the entire review under a spoiler tag. I don’t give away any major plot points or crazy spoilers, but under the spoiler tag I do mention who the hero and heroine is and I set-up the book etc.. Your choice whether you want to click.<br /><br />For those who choose not to read it for now, let me tell you this is one of my absolute favorite reads of the year. Nalini Singh not only has built an incredible world, but she gives us such an intense, dramatic romance. It’s awesome.<br /><br />Onto the review….<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kaleb Krycheck, the dual cardinal with unimaginable power. He easily gets added to my favorite hero list, and honestly – I wasn’t obsessed with him prior to this book as others were. But now that I’ve been in his head, know his story and know the lengths he has gone (and would go) to keep his love safe, I’m blown away. From an extremely young age, the Psy knew Kaleb was very powerful. Taken from his home at the age of three, he was put into a special school for Cardinal Psy. But he didn’t stay there long. Councilor Santano Enrique decided he would be his protégé, and for Kaleb this would change his life in a drastic, evil way. Santano was a serial killer, torturing victim after victim, all the while tearing his way into Kaleb’s mind and body, forcing him to watch, participate and be a part of the extreme evil. This obviously destroys Kaleb. He has one light of hope though. A young girl he happens to meet named Sahara. She is much younger than him, but she becomes his friend as they meet secretly once in awhile. She hugs him one day and he realizes he has never been touched by another human. He falls in love. But when Sahara is sixteen, she is captured, tortured, and kidnapped. <br /><br />Eventually, Kaleb becomes strong enough to get out of Santano’s control, and for the next seven years he searches relentlessly for her. And then he finds her. And he knows, he will never, ever let her go. (And I won’t tell you who has her – but what Kaleb does to this person once he discovers who it is – it’s pretty hardcore. I loved)Sahara is part of the NIghtStar clan (cousin to Faith). While in captivity, she created a labyrinth in her mind, to keep her secrets safe. When Kaleb finds her, she has been tortured and her mind is broken. Very slowly she realizes even though Kaleb has her in a new cage of sorts (his home – he won’t let her go) he is different than her captors. Because her mind is so broken, she doesn’t remember Kaleb or much of anything. Slowly though, she starts to build trust, and her memories start to come back.<br /><br /><i>“Tell me you aren’t evil.” Please.<br />Kaleb’s thumbs moved against he temples. “I’m sorry.”<br /><br />Shaking her head in a mute refusal to accept what he was trying to tell her, she lifted trembling fingers to his jaw. “What have you done?”<br /><br />“Too much that can never be undone.”<br /><br />Crying in earnest now for a man she didn’t know, and yet who was in the most secret part of her heart, she wrapped her arms around his neck and held on, just held on, all the while knowing that he might already have slipped out of her grasp.<br /><br />His arms came around her, locked tight, his breath harsh against her ear. “I’m sorry,” he said again, voice rough as sandpaper and body rigid, as if he’d clenched every muscle he possessed.<br /><br />“It’s okay,” she said through her sobs, “It’s okay.”</i><br /><br /><br />This is what I love about Sahara. Her mind is broken, her memories are only coming to her in pieces, yet inherently she knows Kaleb is not the man Santano made him into be. Kaleb is the most powerful man on the planet, and a girl with a broken mind is the only one that can save him. It’s really beautiful and passionate. Kaleb is so powerful he can not only crack the Earth’s surface with just a thought, but he is strong enough and has plans to either control or destroy the PsyNet. Depending on Sahara, and whether she is ever harmed again, will depend on if the Net gets to live.<br /><br />I could go on and one with the set-up, but let’s get to the good stuff. Kaleb is the most intense, protective hero I’ve read in a long time. The combination of his love (even though he thinks he can’t love) for Sahara and his Silence training, makes me just flail my arms. He is black ice. Nalini Singh gives him insane pent-up emotions, that violently leave his body as he becomes physically active with Sahara. He is her rock, her foundation even though she doesn’t remember him. And as the story unfolds, Sahara becomes his rock. She sees the darkness in him. She understands the horrors he faced with Santano growing up. She is patient, and kind and so loving of him. His love for her – the fact that he finally has her again, is so intense. And he is so tormented, tortured, guilt-ridden, Silent, powerful.<br /><br /><i>Sahara’s eyes were haunted when they met his. “Am I so important to you?”<br /><br />“Yes,” he said. “You’re everything.” The entire reason for his existence.<br /><br />A single tear trailed down Sahara’s cheek. “Why can’t I remember you?”<br /><br />“You’re not strong enough yet.” For the horror, the pain, the realization of the betrayal that had splattered blood around a cheap hotel room when she’d been a girl on the brink of womanhood.<br /><br />Stroking her fingers along his jaw, she said, “Come back, Kaleb.” and stepped closer, moving her hands to his lapels to push the unbuttoned suit jacket off his shoulders. “Walk out of the dark.” </i><br /><br />But in the darkness and among the drama, there are some scenes that will make you smile. Their love is earth shattering. No really.<br /><br /><i>“I just checked the PsyNet,” she said, her own breathing not exactly even. “This region just experienced a medium-sized earthquake.”<br /><br />Kaleb turned his head on the pillow. “It was located deep underground, I made sure of that. No real damage.”</i><br /><br />Oh Kaleb. You literally rocked Sahara’s world.<br /><br />Kaleb and his Arrows are also fighting a war with the PurePsy and their relentless attacks. I really enjoyed how this part of the book played out and how it has been building up through the series. The outcome is pretty awesome as well. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Fans of this series will be blown away by this book. It has been worth the wait. Nalini Singh is an amazing storyteller.<br /><br />Rating: A</span>
  <a data-text-id="17730099772164801619" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }

    }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3147184837402966980">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText3147184837402966980" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
